<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:футболка.html>футбо́лка</a> (20331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:футбол.html>футбо́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">futból</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">football, soccer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:футболка.html>футбо́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">futbólka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:футболка.html>футбо́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:футболка.html>футбо́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:футболка.html>футбо́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>T-shirt <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of shirt</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***фыркать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a> (11140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fýrkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркнуть.html>фы́ркнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to snort, to sniff</li>
<li>to sniff scornfully, to scoff, to grouse, to grumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuckle, to chortle, to snicker</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fýrkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркнуть.html>фы́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fýrknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuckle, to chortle, to snicker</li></ol>

***ха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a> (2214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Cyrillic letter Х, х.</li>
<li>The Roman letter H, h, more often called <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">аш</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>The German letter H, h.</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>Междоме́тие</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ха-</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хаджи.html>хаджи́</a> (27160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хаджи.html>ха́джи</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xádži</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">nominative plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хадж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xadž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

***хаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a> (25928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go somewhere, to visit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>. П. Авенариус, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бродящий.html>Бродя́щие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:современный.html>Совреме́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идиллия.html>иди́ллия</a></i> 1865:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́ю</a> ― <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрекаться.html>отрека́юсь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухаживать.html>уха́живать</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što ja <b>xážival</b> s néju ― ne otrekájusʹ, no <b>xáživatʹ</b> dalekó ješčó ne znáčit uxáživatʹ</i></dd><dd>I do not deny that I <b>visited</b> her, but <b>visiting</b> does not mean wooing</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a> (2126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">خلعت</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hilat</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kaftan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">xələt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dressing gown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uzbek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Uzbek language">Uzbek</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="uz">xalat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">robe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خِلْعَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵilʿa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">robe of honor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xalát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dressing gown, bathrobe (for men or women)</li>
<li>dress (any kind that is knee-length to full and that opens down the front)</li>
<li>smock</li>
<li>surgical gown</li>
<li>oriental robe</li></ol>

***халтура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a> (16893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">chartularius</i>, relating to a chartulary (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хартула́рий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xartulárij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> privy to the imparting of additional earnings. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хавту́ра</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xavtúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хавту́р</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xavtúr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gift to clerics in kind; gift; graft, palm-oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">хаўту́ры</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xaŭtúry</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">funeral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xaltúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now largely unknown</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> funeral banquet, extra-treats in connection to someone being interred
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Pavel_Ivanovich_Melnikov" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:Pavel Ivanovich Melnikov">андре́й пече́рскій</a>,  “Въ лѣса́хъ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Russian_Messenger" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:The Russian Messenger">ру́сскій вѣ́стникъ</a></cite>, volume 98, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=zvsYAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA281">page 281</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Въ <a href = vnd.unilang:поминальный.html>помина́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дни</a> оби́тельски <a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>во́рота</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широко́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крещеный.html>крещёный</a> міръ, <a href = vnd.unilang:распахнутый.html>распа́хнуты</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:немощный.html>не́мощный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> убо́гій — <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кому</a> мѣ́сто <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> столо́м … сберу́тся <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ру</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> „сиро́ты” <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a> съ бѣли́цами изъ захуда́лыхъ <a href = vnd.unilang:обитель.html>оби́телей</a>, приду́тъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> дереве́нскіе христолю́бцы … <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a> свои́хъ сро́дниковъ <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чужи́хъ харча́хъ <a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a>?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V pominálʹnyje dni obítelʹski vorota širokó, na vesʹ kreščónyj mir, raspáxnuty — pridí sílʹnyj, pridí némoščnyj, pridí bogátyj, pridí ubógij — vsjákomu mě́sto za stolóm … Sberútsja na <b>xaltúru</b> i „siróty” i máteri s bělícami iz zaxudályx obítelej, pridút i derevénskije xristoljúbcy … Komú ne oxóta svoíx sródnikov na čužíx xarčáx pomjanútʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In funeral days the monasterial doors are flung open widely, to all the christened word – it may come the strong, it may come the powerless, it may come the wretched – to everyone there is a place before the table … to the <b>banquet</b> gather even the “orphans” and mothers with nuns from the abandoned cloisters, come even the rural Christ-lovers … Who does not want to commemorate his relatives on someone else’s catering?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминки.html>поми́нки</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomínki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yields acquired or work performed irregularly, job of imperfect compliance
<ol><li>undeclared work, black market job, supplementary contract, moonlighting, participation in informal economy; khaltura
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1857</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%98%D0%BB%D1%8C%D1%8F_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Илья Васильевич Селиванов">илья́ васи́льевич селива́нов</a></span>,  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провинціа́льныя воспомина́нія. <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:записка.html>запи́сок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудак.html>чудака́</a></span></cite>, Moscow, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=R80NAAAAIAAJamp;pg=PA67">pages 67–68</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">стря́пчйі<sup style="font-style:normal">[<i>sic</i>]</sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> зналъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> испра́вникъ <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жный</a> человѣ́къ; <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всюду.html>всю́ду</a>, гдѣ стря́пчему быва́етъ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></b>, испра́вникъ мо́жетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>отня́ть</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Strjápčji<sup style="font-style:normal">[<i>sic</i>]</sup> tóže óčenʹ xorošó znal, što isprávnik jemú núžnyj čelově́k; što vsjúdu, gdě strjápčemu byvájet <b>xaltúra</b>, isprávnik móžet jejó u nevó otnjátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Stryapchiy knew well too, that he needs the Ispravnik; that everywhere where the Stryapchiy gets an <b>extra-earning</b>, the Ispravnik might take it away from him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  G Wylx (lyrics),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пацан.html>пацаны́</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Джизнь</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ре</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёбе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ре</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:физкультура.html>физкульту́ре</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ре</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> гламу́ре<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:пацан.html>пацаны́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Po rabóte, po kulʹtúre, i v učóbe i v amúre<br />V fizkulʹtúre, i v <b>xaltúre</b>, i v glamúre<br />Pacaný</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In work, in culture, and in studies and in love<br />In sport, and in moonlighting, and in glamor<br />Boys</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>shoddy work (something intentionally done badly), botched job, bungled job; hack; a botch; a pot boiler; khaltura
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> September 17,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BD%D1%8F%D0%B5%D0%B2,_%D0%90%D0%BD%D0%B4%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%AE%D1%80%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Коняев, Андрей Юрьевич">андре́й коня́ев</a></span>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыносимый.html>невыноси́мая</a> втори́чность <a href = vnd.unilang:бытие.html>бытия́</a>. андре́й коня́ев <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ре</a>, алекса́ндре <a href = vnd.unilang:невский.html>не́вском</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> дели́рии</span>”, in  <cite>Lenta.ru</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lenta.ru/columns/2011/09/17/jesus/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говоримый.html>говори́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> бл*, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подозревать.html>подозрева́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чило</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круго́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сплошной.html>сплошна́я</a> втори́чность <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My že govorím o Ródine! No bl*, ja štó-to takóje užé davnó podozrevál, múčilo menjá čúvstvo, što krugóm splošnája vtoríčnostʹ i <b>xaltúra</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We're talking about the Motherland, you know! But f*ck, I have long suspected something like that, I had a hurting feeling that everything around is sheer secondariness and a <b>hack job</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ля.html>ля́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-халяв-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***хам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>хам</a> (11145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>Хам</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Xam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - biblical character.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>хам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xam</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boor, cad (сrass, impudent, ill-bred man), asshole</li></ol>

***хамство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хамство.html>ха́мство</a> (10047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>хам</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хамство.html>ха́мство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xámstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хамство.html>ха́мства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хамство.html>ха́мства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хамство.html>ха́мств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boorishness, rudeness, loutishness; chutzpah</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́м</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-хам-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ств</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b>.
</p>

***хан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>хан</a> (5031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolic languages">Mongolic</a></span> source, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolian language">Mongolian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mn"><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>хаан</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">haan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from the same <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кага́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kagán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>A possible intermediary is <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chagatai_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chagatai language">Chagatai</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="chg">خان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="chg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
